	$.ajax({
		url: 'index.php?route=common/header/login',
		type: 'post',
		data: $('#ajax-login :input'),
		dataType: 'json',
		beforeSend: function() {
			$('#button-ajax-login').attr('disabled', true);
			$('#button-ajax-login').before('<span class="wait">&nbsp;<img src="catalog/view/theme/WD/img/loading.gif" alt="" /></span>');
		},
		complete: function() {
			$('#button-ajax-login').attr('disabled', false);
			$('#ajax-login .wait').remove();
		},
		success: function(json) {
			$('#ajax-login #ajax-error').remove();

			if (json['error']) {

				$('#ajax-login .content').prepend('<div id="ajax-error" style="display: none;">' + json['error']['warning'] + '</div>');

				$('#ajax-error').fadeIn('slow');

			} else {

				var redirect = 'https://www.winedirect.co.uk/';
				location = redirect.replace(/\&amp;/g, '&');

			}
		}
	});
});
